async function ic(e, t) {
    let {data: n, response: r, error: i} = await Et.GET(`/rest/sources/${encodeURIComponent(e)}`, t, {
        normalizedPath: `/rest/sources/{source_id}`
    });
    if (i || !n)
        throw new we(`API_CLIENTS_ERROR`,{
            message: `Failed to fetch source ${e}`,
            cause: i,
            status: r.status ?? 0
        });
    return n
}
function ac(e) {
    return typeof e == `object` && !!e && !Array.isArray(e) && `pages`in e && Array.isArray(e.pages)
}
function oc(e) {
    return typeof e == `object` && !!e && `sources`in e && Array.isArray(e.sources)
}
function sc(e) {
    return typeof e == `object` && !!e && `id`in e && typeof e.id == `string` && `display_name`in e && typeof e.display_name == `string` && `description`in e && typeof e.description == `string` && `type`in e && typeof e.type == `string`
}
function cc(e, t) {
    let n = e.getQueryCache()
      , r = hn()
      , i = n.findAll({
        queryKey: r,
        exact: !1
    });
    for (let e of i) {
        let n = e.state.data;
        if (n) {
            if (ac(n)) {
                for (let e of n.pages)
                    if (oc(e)) {
                        let n = e.sources.find(e => sc(e) && e.id === t);
                        if (n)
                            return n
                    }
            }
            if (sc(n) && n.id === t)
                return n
        }
    }
    return null
}

    merge: {

function Rc(e, t) {
    if (t && t in Lc)
        return !0;
    if (!e)
        return !1;
    let {bullets: n, connected_bullets: r, consumer_bullets: i, developer: a, website_url: o, documentation_url: s, support_url: c, footnote: l} = e;
    return !!(n?.length || r?.length || i?.length || o || s || c || l || a)
}
function zc({sourceDetails: e, connectorName: t, connectionStatus: n, isEnterprise: r, displayName: i, description: a, provider: o}) {
    let s = [];
    e.website_url && s.push({
        label: `Website`,
        url: e.website_url,
        icon: _(`link`)
    }),
    e.documentation_url && s.push({
        label: `Documentation`,
        url: e.documentation_url,
        icon: _(`book`)
    }),
    e.support_url && s.push({
        label: `Support`,
        url: e.support_url,
        icon: _(`help`)
    });
    let c = e.bullets ?? [];
    n === Mc.CONNECTED && e.connected_bullets?.length ? c = e.connected_bullets : !r && e.consumer_bullets?.length && (c = e.consumer_bullets);
    let l = e.footnote ?? (o ? Lc[o] ?? null : null);
    return {
        name: i || Tr(t),
        tagline: a ?? null,
        footnote: l,
        bullets: [...c],
        links: s,
        developer: e.developer ?? null
    }
}
var Bc = (e, t=Mc.DISCONNECTED, n, r, i) => {
    let {$t: a} = X()
      , o = Te()
      , s = wn()

    Q.useMemo)( () => s?.find(t => t.id === e), [s, e])

    return (0,
    Q.useMemo)( () => {
        let r = n?.source_details;
        if (r && Rc(r, l))
            return zc({

            });

              , g = [{
                label: `Website`,
                url: i,
                icon: _(`link`)
            }];
            c && g.push({
                label: `Documentation`,
                url: c,
                icon: _(`book`)
            }),
            u && g.push({
                label: `Support`,
                url: u,
                icon: _(`help`)
            });
            let v = p;
            return t === Mc.CONNECTED && m ? v = m : !o && f && (v = f),
            {
                name: n?.display_name || r || Tr(e),
                tagline: l ? a(l) : null,
                footnote: d ? {
                    link: d.link,
                    text: a(d.text)
                } : null,
                bullets: v.map(e => a(e)),
                links: g,
                developer: a(h)
            }

function Cm(e, t) {

    case `SET_EXPANDED`:
        return {
            ...e,
            isExpanded: t.payload
        };

        return {
            ...e,
            isActive: t.payload
        };
    case `SET_COMPOSING`:
        return {
            ...e,
            isComposing: t.payload
        };
    default:
        return e
    }
}

function Nm() {
    return !document.activeElement?.closest(`[role="tablist"]`)
}
function Pm(e) {
    if (va(e, ClipboardEvent))
        return e.clipboardData;
    if (va(e, InputEvent))
        return e.dataTransfer;
    if (`clipboardData`in e) {
        let t = e.clipboardData;
        if (t instanceof DataTransfer)
            return t
    }
    if (`dataTransfer`in e) {
        let t = e.dataTransfer;
        if (t instanceof DataTransfer)
            return t
    }
    return null
}

function Bm() {
    let e = ma();
    if (e.getChildrenSize() <= 1)
        return;
    let t = e.getChildren()
      , n = t[0];
    if (ja(n))
        for (let e = 1; e < t.length; e++) {
            let r = t[e];
            if (no(r)) {
                n.append(Ya());
                for (let e of r.getChildren())
                    (Aa(e) || Oa(e) || Xa(e) || da(e)) && n.append(e);
                r.remove()
            }
        }
}

function Hm(e) {
